  â”‚   â”‚       â”† class WebSocketService {

  â”‚   â”‚       â”†

  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     if (!token) return;

  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ´ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ÑÑ Ğº Ğ²ĞµĞ±ÑĞ¾ĞºĞµÑ‚Ñƒ Ğ±ÑĞºĞµĞ½Ğ´Ğ°
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     const host = window.location.host;
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     this.ws = new WebSocket(`ws://${host}/api/v1/notifications/ws?token=${token}`);
  â”‚   â”‚       â”† 
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     this.ws.onopen = () => {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       console.log('ğŸŸ¢ WS Connected');
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     };
  â”‚   â”‚       â”† 
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     this.ws.onmessage = (event) => {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       try {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†         const message = JSON.parse(event.data);
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†         console.log('ğŸ“© WS Message:', message);
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†         // Ğ Ğ°ÑÑÑ‹Ğ»Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ²ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑÑ‡Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ğ¼
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†         this.handlers.forEach(handler => handler(message));
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       } catch (e) {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†         console.error('WS Parse Error', e);
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       }
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     };
  â”‚   â”‚       â”† 
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     this.ws.onclose = () => {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       console.log('ğŸ”´ WS Disconnected');
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       // ĞœĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾-Ñ€ĞµĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ğ½ĞµĞºÑ‚, Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ĞºÑƒÑ€ÑĞ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ñ…Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‚ Ğ¸ Ñ‚Ğ°Ğº
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     };
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†   }
  â”‚   â”‚       â”† 
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†   subscribe(handler: MessageHandler) {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     this.handlers.push(handler);
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     // Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ¸
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     return () => {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       this.handlers = this.handlers.filter(h => h !== handler);
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     };
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†   }
  â”‚   â”‚       â”† 
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†   disconnect() {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     if (this.ws) {
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       this.ws.close();
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†       this.ws = null;
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†     }
  â”‚   â”‚       â”†   }
  â”‚   â”‚       â”† }

  â”‚       â”‚   â”† import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† import { api } from '../api/client';
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† import { wsService } from '../api/websocket';
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† import { GridMap } from '../components/GridMap';

  â”‚       â”‚   â”† export const DriverPage = ({ onBack }: { onBack: () => void }) => {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const [isOnline, setIsOnline] = useState(false);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const [location, setLocation] = useState({ x: 50, y: 50 });
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const [status, setStatus] = useState('offline');
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const [lastUpdate, setLastUpdate] = useState<string>('-');
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† 
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const [activeRide, setActiveRide] = useState<any>(null);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const [incomingOrder, setIncomingOrder] = useState<any>(null);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† 
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   // Ğ’Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ĞºĞ¾Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‚
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const updateCoord = (axis: 'x' | 'y', value: string) => {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     let val = parseInt(value);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     if (isNaN(val)) val = 0;
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     val = Math.max(0, Math.min(99, val));
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     setLocation(prev => ({ ...prev, [axis]: val }));
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   };
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† 
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   useEffect(() => {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     let intervalId: any;
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     const sendHeartbeat = async () => {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       try {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         await api.put('/drivers/me/presence', {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†           status: 'online',
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†           location: { x: Number(location.x), y: Number(location.y) }
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         });
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         setLastUpdate(new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         setStatus('online');
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       } catch (e) { setStatus('error'); }
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     };
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† 
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     if (isOnline) {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       sendHeartbeat();
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       intervalId = setInterval(sendHeartbeat, 3000);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† 
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       // WebSocket Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ´ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       wsService.connect();
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       const unsubscribe = wsService.subscribe((msg) => {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         if (msg.type === 'NEW_ORDER_PROPOSAL') {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†           console.log("ğŸ”” ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·:", msg.data);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†           setIncomingOrder(msg.data);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         }
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       });
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† 
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       return () => {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         clearInterval(intervalId);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         unsubscribe();
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†         wsService.disconnect();
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       };
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     } else {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       setStatus('offline');
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     }
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   }, [isOnline, location]);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”† 
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†   const handleAcceptOrder = async () => {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     if (!incomingOrder) return;
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     try {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       const res = await api.post(`/rides/${incomingOrder.ride_id}/accept`);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       setActiveRide(res.data);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       setIncomingOrder(null);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     } catch (e) {
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       alert("ĞĞµ ÑƒĞ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾ÑÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·.");
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†       setIncomingOrder(null);
  â”‚       â”‚   â”†     }

  â”‚           â”† import { api } from '../api/client';
  â”‚           â”† import { GridMap } from '../components/GridMap';
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”† export const PassengerPage = ({ onBack }: { onBack: () => void }) => {
  â”‚           â”†   const [step, setStep] = useState<'select_start' | 'select_end' | 'ready' | 'ordered' | 'completed'>('select_start');
  â”‚           â”†   const [pickup, setPickup] = useState<{ x: number, y: number } | null>(null);
  â”‚           â”†   const [destination, setDestination] = useState<{ x: number, y: number } | null>(null);
  â”‚           â”†   const [rideInfo, setRideInfo] = useState<any>(null);
  â”‚           â”†   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  â”‚           â”†   const [rating, setRating] = useState(0);
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†   // ĞĞ’Ğ¢Ğ-ĞĞ‘ĞĞĞ’Ğ›Ğ•ĞĞ˜Ğ• Ğ¡Ğ¢ĞĞ¢Ğ£Ğ¡Ğ
  â”‚           â”†   useEffect(() => {
  â”‚           â”†     let interval: any;
  â”‚           â”†     if (step === 'ordered' && rideInfo?.ride_id) {
  â”‚           â”†       interval = setInterval(async () => {
  â”‚           â”†         try {
  â”‚           â”†           const res = await api.get('/rides/history');
  â”‚           â”†           const myRides = res.data;
  â”‚           â”†           // Ğ‘ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ»ĞµĞ´Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¹ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ· Ñ Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºĞ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¶Ğµ ID
  â”‚           â”†           const currentRide = myRides.find((r: any) => r.ride_id === rideInfo.ride_id);
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†           if (currentRide) {
  â”‚           â”†             setRideInfo(currentRide);
  â”‚           â”†             if (currentRide.status === 'completed') {
  â”‚           â”†               setStep('completed');
  â”‚           â”†               clearInterval(interval);
  â”‚           â”†             }
  â”‚           â”†           }
  â”‚           â”†         } catch (e) {
  â”‚           â”†           console.error(e);
  â”‚           â”†         }
  â”‚           â”†       }, 2000);
  â”‚           â”†     }
  â”‚           â”†     return () => clearInterval(interval);
  â”‚           â”†   }, [step, rideInfo]);
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†   const handleMapClick = (x: number, y: number) => {
  â”‚           â”†     if (step === 'select_start') {
  â”‚           â”†       setPickup({ x, y });
  â”‚           â”†       setStep('select_end');
  â”‚           â”†     } else if (step === 'select_end') {
  â”‚           â”†       setDestination({ x, y });
  â”‚           â”†       setStep('ready');
  â”‚           â”†     }
  â”‚           â”†   };
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†   const handleOrder = async () => {
  â”‚           â”†     if (!pickup || !destination) return;
  â”‚           â”†     setLoading(true);
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†     // ĞŸĞ Ğ•ĞĞ‘Ğ ĞĞ—Ğ£Ğ•Ğœ Ğ’ Ğ§Ğ˜Ğ¡Ğ›Ğ, Ğ§Ğ¢ĞĞ‘Ğ« Ğ˜Ğ—Ğ‘Ğ•Ğ–ĞĞ¢Ğ¬ ĞĞ¨Ğ˜Ğ‘ĞšĞ˜ 422
  â”‚           â”†     const payload = {
  â”‚           â”†       start_x: Number(pickup.x),
  â”‚           â”†       start_y: Number(pickup.y),
  â”‚           â”†       end_x: Number(destination.x),
  â”‚           â”†       end_y: Number(destination.y)
  â”‚           â”†     };
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†     try {
  â”‚           â”†       const response = await api.post('/rides', payload);
  â”‚           â”†       setRideInfo(response.data);
  â”‚           â”†       setStep('ordered');
  â”‚           â”†     } catch (error: any) {
  â”‚           â”†       console.error(error);
  â”‚           â”†       if (error.response?.status === 422) {
  â”‚           â”†         alert("ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…. ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑŒÑ‚Ğµ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½ÑĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒ.");
  â”‚           â”†       } else {

  â”‚           â”†       }
  â”‚           â”†     } finally {
  â”‚           â”†       setLoading(false);
  â”‚           â”†     }
  â”‚           â”†   };
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†   const handleReset = () => {
  â”‚           â”†     setPickup(null);
  â”‚           â”†     setDestination(null);
  â”‚           â”†     setRideInfo(null);
  â”‚           â”†     setRating(0);
  â”‚           â”†     setStep('select_start');
  â”‚           â”†   };
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†   const submitRating = () => {
  â”‚           â”†     alert(`Ğ¡Ğ¿Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ±Ğ¾ Ğ·Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ†ĞµĞ½ĞºÑƒ ${rating} Ğ·Ğ²ĞµĞ·Ğ´!`);
  â”‚           â”†     handleReset();
  â”‚           â”†   };
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†   const getStatusColor = (s: string) => {
  â”‚           â”†     switch(s) {
  â”‚           â”†       case 'pending': return 'text-orange-500';
  â”‚           â”†       case 'driver_assigned': return 'text-blue-600';
  â”‚           â”†       case 'driver_arrived': return 'text-purple-600';

  â”‚           â”†       case 'completed': return 'text-gray-800';
  â”‚           â”†       default: return 'text-gray-500';
  â”‚           â”†     }
  â”‚           â”†   };
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†   return (
  â”‚           â”†     <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100 p-4 md:p-8">
  â”‚           â”†       <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto mb-6">
  â”‚           â”†         <button onClick={onBack} className="bg-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-sm hover:shadow-md text-gray-700">â† ĞĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ´</button>
  â”‚           â”†       </div>
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†       <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-8">
  â”‚           â”† 
  â”‚           â”†         {/* ĞšĞĞ Ğ¢Ğ */}
  â”‚           â”†         <div className="lg:col-span-2 bg-white p-6 rounded-3xl shadow-xl min-h-[500px] flex flex-col items-center">
  â”‚           â”†           <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800 mb-4 self-start">
  â”‚           â”†             {step === 'select_start' && "ğŸ“ Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 1: Ğ’Ñ‹Ğ±ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡ĞºÑƒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ¸ (ĞÑ‚ĞºÑƒĞ´Ğ°?)"}
  â”‚           â”†             {step === 'select_end' && "ğŸ Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 2: Ğ’Ñ‹Ğ±ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ¿ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ‚ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ (ĞšÑƒĞ´Ğ°?)"}
  â”‚           â”†             {(step === 'ready' || step === 'ordered') && "ğŸ—ºï¸ ĞœĞ°Ñ€ÑˆÑ€ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞ½"}
